<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Khanapara Teer Result</strong></h2>



<!-- 728x90/300x250/320x50/468x60 -->
<div id="waldo-tag-24245"></div>



<p>The Khanapara Teer game, legally hosted in the Meghalaya border area near East Khanapara of the RiBhoi district, is a traditional archery competition. ThemMarwet, a coalition of 12 archery clubs from the area, organizes it. During each session, 50 archers shoot between 300 to 1000 arrows, with the score determined by the last two digits of the total arrows that hit the target. For instance, if 650 arrows strike the target, the score recorded is 50.</p>



<p>You can check the Khanapara Teer Results Today here.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Shillong Teer Direct/Single Number</strong></h2>



<p>It is the dream of every Shillong local to earn a jackpot and become rich in a short time, but this is a matter of luck and some calculation. People are stuck in the teer game by losing their ticket money daily. Therefore, a direct number should be selected carefully. The direct number is called a&nbsp;<strong>single number</strong>, the anticipated winning number. If you guess the number correctly, you will win the game.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Precautions for Teer Game</strong></h2>



<!-- 728x90/300x250/320x50/468x60 -->
<div id="waldo-tag-24247"></div>



<p>Teer of Shillong is the addiction of Shillong’s people. The game is so intriguing that no one can resist playing it daily. Since the game’s structure is based on gambling, there are high chances of losing a large amount of money now and then. So it is a risky lottery.</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>It is recommended not to play the lottery every day, don’t buy the tickets based on your loan amount, and calculate the dream/ common number before you play a round because it can make you rich or poor in a single day.&nbsp;</li>



<li>Don’t fall for the greed of winning more and more. If you aggressively put yourself into this game, you may lose the consciousness to play strategically.</li>



<li>Don’t trust someone online who offers you winning numbers. Don’t give any money over WhatsApp or Facebook.</li>



<li>You must be over eighteen years old to understand the game’s strategy unless it will be hard to refrain from losing your valued money.</li>
</ul>

These important figures help locals win an <a href="https://trackingstatus.in/st-courier-tracking/" rel="noopener">ST Courier package</a> daily.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>FAQs</strong></h2>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-accordion alignnone"><div class="kt-accordion-wrap kt-accordion-id10566_74b995-1f kt-accordion-has-3-panes kt-active-pane-0 kt-accordion-block kt-pane-header-alignment-left kt-accodion-icon-style-basic kt-accodion-icon-side-right" style="max-width:none"><div class="kt-accordion-inner-wrap" data-allow-multiple-open="false" data-start-open="0">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-1 kt-pane10566_b8fa71-7d"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What is the House and the Ending numbers?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The Teeter game is played by betting on a two-digit number. A two-digit first digit is called the &#8220;house number,&#8221; and its last digit is known as the &#8220;ending number.&#8221;</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane10566_9f3bcb-f3"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What is the meaning of Shillong Teer?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Shillong is a hill area in northwest India. It is the capital of the state of Meghalaya, whereas a teer is called an arrow in English. There is an archery game played in Shillong city which involves arrow shooting. Therefore, the Shillong Teer is the game of teer played in Shillong.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane10566_f9da9c-25"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What are FR and SR in Teer?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>In the Teer game, there are two rounds played. The first round is known as F/R, and the second round is known as S/R.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div></div></div>



<p><a href="https://teerwin.com/shillong-teer-prediction-today/"></a></p>
